!-------------- Advertising networks ---------------------------------------!
! This section contains the list of third-party advertising networks domains for mobile devices.
! Note, that we only put rules that block full domains here and not URL parts (there's `general_url.txt` for that). Also, it must be domains that are used in a third-party context.
! Good: ||doubleclick.net^$third-party
! Bad: /banner.jpg (should be in general_url.txt)
! Bad: ||adssubdomain.legitwebsite.com^ (should be in adservers_firstparty.txt)
! ||mobileapptracking.com^ - don't block this domain with all subdomains. https://forum.adguard.com/index.php?threads/23917/

!-------------- Anti-adblock rules -----------------------------------------!
! First of all, this section has common rules that prevent most known ad block detections. In that case domain should be added to the common rules.
! The section contains the list of the rules are against all kinds of ads reinjection or ad-blocking circumvention scripts. If such a script does not cripple the website, we add rules to the Annoyances filter.
! Rules should generally be domain-specific. In some exceptional cases, it's allowed to add generic ones, but this should be approved by most of the maintainers.
! Good: ||example.org/adblock/detect.js
! Good: @@/adblocker/detect.js$domain=example.org
! Bad: ||ad.doubleclick.net^ (should be in adservers.txt)

!-------------- General javascript, CSS and HTML extensions ----------------!
! This section contains the list of ad blocking rules that fall under "advanced" category.
! By advanced we mean the following rule types: CSS, scriptlets, HTML filtering (`$$` marker), JS.
! Good: example.org#$##rek { display: none !important; }; example.org#%#//scriptlet('set-cookie', 'ad', '0'); example.org$$script[tag-content="ad"][max-length="3000"].
! Bad: example.org###rek (should be in specific.txt)

!-------------- General URL blocking rules ---------------------------------!
! This section contains the list of generic blocking rules (mobile sites or apps).
! Good: .org/ads/
! Bad: .org/ads/$domain=example.org (for instance, should be in speficic.txt)
||cloudads-a.akamaihd.net^
! For blocking ads in mobile apps with HTTPS filtering on Android
! Facebook Ad Choices
! Yandex Ads

!-------------- Rules for specific websites --------------------------------!
! This section contains the list of domain-specific rules that block ads on mobile devices.
! Good: example.org###rek; ||m.example.com/ads/
! Bad: example.org#@##banner_ad (for instance, should be in allowlist.txt or in antiadblock.txt)
! https://forum.adguard.com/index.php?threads/10464/
! Facebook
!! old interface
!! new interface
!! new interface search ads
!!! Ad in menu
! For iPad - it has a different layout than smaller devices
! Common names
! ##amp-embed[type="outbrain"]
! ##amp-embed[type="taboola"]
! ##amp-ad
! ##.ads
! ##.ad
! ##.Ad
! ##body .banner

! Title: AWAvenue 秋风广告规则（AWAvenue-Ads-Rule-Replenish）
! 规则版本: 0.0.1-beta
! 更新时间: 2024-08-28
! 项目地址：https://github.com/TG-Twilight/AWAvenue-Ads-Rule
! 如果需要在其它规则中混合此规则，请在您的规则显眼处注明本规则的出处，谢谢！
! 加入Telegram群组 秋風がく山道 (@AWAvenueAdsChat) 与编写者交流，期待着您的到来！
! 群组链接：https://t.me/AWAvenueAdsChat
! 订阅Telegram频道 AWAvenue Ads Rule (@AWAvenueAdsRule) 获取最新公告，期待着您的订阅！
! 频道链接：https://t.me/AWAvenueAdsRule
! This project is licensed under the Attribution-NonCommercial-ShareAlike 4.0 International (CC BY-NC-SA 4.0) license.
! 倾城极速 - 畅游世界，高速互联！官网：https://wcnmdmht.lol/sb 官网2：https://panel.qc02.xyz
! 此为“秋风广告规则（AWAvenue-Ads-Rule）”的补充规则，请与“秋风广告规则（AWAvenue-Ads-Rule）”配合使用！
! 此规则包含了一些较为激进的被拦截域名（激进程度远远不如“AWAvenue-Ads-Rule-Strict激进版”），且每个都配有相关的说明。
! 这些域名通常来讲不会太影响你网络的正常使用，但还是为有需要的人提供了一个选择，你可以自由选择是否订阅。
# 用于拦截 WeChat 的ads请求，开启后对于 WeChat 的订阅号拦截会相当激进。
||acs.m.taobao.com^
# 用于拦截 Taobao 的强制更新，开启后部分 Ali 系产品的某些服务可能异常（如Ali Drive的登录验证码之类）。
||contentcenter-drcn.dbankcdn.cn^
||h5hosting.dbankcdn.com^
# 用于拦截 Whyway 天气的开屏广告，拦截后，会导致花瓣测速无法获取测速服务器列表、Whyway运动健康图片 资源无法加载等情况。
/i*.snssdk.com/
||i*.snssdk.com^
# 用于拦截 zijie 系的广告，拦截后，会导致抖音APP的填写学校->学校信息->申报学校信息异常。
||weather-drcn.music.dbankcloud.cn^
# 用于拦截 Whyway 天气的开屏广告，拦截后，可能会导致 更多天气加载失败 等情况。
||mcdn.bilivideo.cn^
# 用于拦截睿站的pcdn上传行为，启用后将会使用bilibili自己的视频cdn节点，但同时可能会导致视频播放时弹出验证码等诸如此类的情况。
||staticsns.cdn.bcebos.com^
# 用于拦截 baidu Netdisk 部分资源的错误拦截（经核实，该域名为正常内容与广告内容混用链接）。
||analytics.95516.com^
# 用于拦截一些追踪行为，但是会导致某些app中的部分页面无法打开（例如云闪付的国补），故移动至此处。
||p2p.huya.com^
# 用于拦截虎牙直播的上传行为，但部分线路依赖此行为，好吧，它现在被挪到这里了。
||static.wxqcloud.qq.com.cn^
# 用于拦截 WeChat 订阅号中的特殊广告，但部小程序依赖此域名加载css，well, he's here now.
||hismarttv.com^
# 用于拦截 Hisense TV 的广告和云控，但部分正常资源也依赖此加载，所以，它现在到这里来了。
||open-iflow.meizu.com^
||reader.meizu.com^
||dw-reader.meizu.com^
# 用于拦截魅族手机Flyme系统内置天气app二级页面中的低质推广资讯，但该内容并非广告，故添加于此。
